[See also art. <foreign lang="ar">قر</foreign>.])          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">صاب</foreign>, aor. as above, (M, TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">صَوْبٌ</foreign>, (K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">It,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">he, came from a high place;</hi> (K, TA;) <hi rend="ital">descended from above;</hi> (M, TA;) as also

                     <itype>2</itype>        
                     <orth lang="ar">صَوَّبَ</orth>
                  </form> see above, last sentence but one.          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence, app.,] <foreign lang="ar">صَوَّبْتُ الفَرَسَ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">I sent forth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">started,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">let go, the horse in running.</hi> (S, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">تَصْوِيبٌ</foreign> is the <hi rend="ital">contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">تَصْعِيدٌ</foreign> [generally in a trans. sense (though also in an intrans. sense as will be seen below); i. e. it signifies The <hi rend="ital">making to descend</hi>]. (M, TA.) One says, <foreign lang="ar">صوّب رَأْسَهُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He lowered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">depressed, his head.</hi> (S, A, Mgh, Msb, K.) And <foreign lang="ar">صَوَّبَ ٱللّٰهُ رَأْسَهُ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">May God degrade him;</hi> lit.] <hi rend="ital">may God lower,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">depress, his head.</hi> (TA.) It is said in a trad., <foreign lang="ar">مَنْ قَطَعَ سِدْرَةً</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">صَوَّبَ ٱللّٰهُ رَأْسَهُ فِى النَّارِ</foreign>, which, accord. to Aboo-Dáwood Es-Sijistánee, is abridged, and means, <hi rend="ital">Whoso cuts down,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">lops, a</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">سدرة</foreign> [which is a species of lote-tree], in a desert, by the shade whereof the traveller shelters himself, without just cause, <hi rend="ital">God will,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">may God, lower his head</hi> [<hi rend="ital">in the fire</hi> of Hell]. (L, TA.) And one says, <foreign lang="ar">صوّب يَدَهُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He lowered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">depressed, his hand,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">arm.</hi> (L, TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">صوّب الإِنَآءَ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He inclined the vessel</hi> (Mgh, Msb) <hi rend="ital">downwards, in order that what was in it might run</hi> [<hi rend="ital">out</hi>]: (Mgh:) or <hi rend="ital">he lowered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">depressed, the vessel;</hi> and in like manner, <foreign lang="ar">رَأْسَ الخَشَبَةِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">the head of the piece of wood</hi>]. (T, TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">صوّب إِلَيْهِ يَصَرَهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He directed his sight towards him</hi>]. (Msb in art. <foreign lang="ar">لمح</foreign>. [From <foreign lang="ar">الصَّوَابُ</foreign>.]) And <foreign lang="ar">صَعَّدَ فِىَّ النَّظَرَ وَصَوَّبَهُ</foreign>: see art. <foreign lang="ar">صعد</foreign>.          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">صَوَّبْتُ قَوْلَهُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">I said that his saying was</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">صَوَاب</foreign> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">right;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">I pronounced his saying to be right</hi>]. (Msb.) And <foreign lang="ar">صوّب رَأْيَهُ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">He pronounced his opinion to be right</hi>]. (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">صوّبهُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He said to him</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَصَبْتَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Thou hast hit the right thing;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">said,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">done, right</hi>]. (S, K.)
